   <!-- //20180327 mstar -->
   <style>
    .main-hero .lslide {background-color:#f9f9f9;}
   </style>
   <script type="text/javascript">
    $(function(){
 
 	// 메인 상단 롤링
 	$(".main-hero").each(function() {
 
 		var $ui = $(this);
 		var $tabCate = $ui.find(".tabmenu > ul > li");
 		var $tabItem = $ui.find(".tabmenu dd li");
 		var lSlider = $ui.find(".list ul").lightSlider({
 			item: 1,
 			mode: "fade",
 			loop: true,
 			pager: false,
 			controls: false,
 			auto: true,
 			pause: 3000,
 			//pauseOnHover:true,
 			enableTouch:false,
 			enableDrag:false,
 			onSliderLoad: function() {
 				$ui.find(".list").css({ visibility: "inherit" });
 				set_page();
 			},
 			onBeforeSlide: function() {
 				var $item = $tabItem.eq(lSlider.getCurrentSlideCount() - 1).parent().find("li").removeClass("on")
 				.end().end().addClass("on");
 				var index = $tabCate.index($tabCate.has($item));
 				$tabCate.removeClass("on").eq(index).addClass("on");
 				set_page();
 			}
 		});
 
 		$tabCate.on("mouseenter mouseleave", function(_e) {
 			switch(_e.type) {
 				case "mouseenter":
 					$(this).addClass("open");
 					if ($(this).find(".on").length == 0) $(this).find("dd li").eq(0).trigger("mouseenter");
 					else lSlider.goToSlide($tabItem.index($(this).find(".on")) + 1);
 				break;
 				case "mouseleave":
 					$(this).removeClass("open");
 				break;
 			}
 		});
 
 		$tabItem.on("mouseenter", function(_e) {
 			lSlider.goToSlide($tabItem.index(this) + 1);
 		});
 
 		$ui.find(".btn_prev").on("click", function(_e) {
 			_e.preventDefault();
 			lSlider.goToPrevSlide();
 		});
 
 		$ui.find(".btn_next").on("click", function(_e) {
 			_e.preventDefault();
 			lSlider.goToNextSlide();
 		});
 
 		$ui.find(".btn_toggle").on("click", function(_e) {
 			_e.preventDefault();
 			$(this).toggleClass("on");
 			if ($(this).hasClass("on")) lSlider.pause();
 			else {
 				lSlider.goToPrevSlide();
 				lSlider.play();
 			}
 		});
 
 		$ui.find(".new_container").on("mouseenter mouseleave", function(_e) {
 			switch(_e.type) {
 				case "mouseenter":
 					lSlider.pause();
 				break;
 				case "mouseleave":
 					if (!$ui.find(".btn_toggle").hasClass("on")) {
 						lSlider.goToPrevSlide();
 						lSlider.play();
 					}
 				break;
 			}
 		});
 
 		function set_page() {
 			$ui.find(".page > .current").text(lSlider.getCurrentSlideCount()).end()
 			.find(".page > .total").text(lSlider.getTotalSlideCount());
 		}
 
 		$(".main-hero div.tabmenu > ul > li:nth-child(2)").trigger("mouseenter").trigger("mouseleave");
 
 	});
 	// 메인 상단 롤링
 
 
 	// 메인 띠배너 롤링
 	$(".main-banner").each(function() {
 
 		var $ui = $(this);
 		var lSlider = $ui.children("ul").lightSlider({
 			item: 1,
 			mode: "fade",
 			loop: true,
 			pager: false,
 			controls: false,
 			auto: true,
 			pause: 3000,
 			//pauseOnHover:true,
 			enableTouch:false,
 			enableDrag:false,
 			onSliderLoad: set_page,
 			onBeforeSlide: set_page
 		});
 
 		$ui.find(".btn_prev").on("click", function(_e) {
 			_e.preventDefault();
 			lSlider.goToPrevSlide();
 		});
 
 		$ui.find(".btn_next").on("click", function(_e) {
 			_e.preventDefault();
 			lSlider.goToNextSlide();
 		});
 
 		$ui.find(".btn_toggle").on("click", function(_e) {
 			_e.preventDefault();
 			$(this).toggleClass("on");
 			if ($(this).hasClass("on")) lSlider.pause();
 			else {
 				lSlider.goToPrevSlide();
 				lSlider.play();
 			}
 		});
 
 		$ui.on("mouseenter mouseleave", function(_e) {
 			switch(_e.type) {
 				case "mouseenter":
 					lSlider.pause();
 				break;
 				case "mouseleave":
 					if (!$ui.find(".btn_toggle").hasClass("on")) {
 						lSlider.goToPrevSlide();
 						lSlider.play();
 					}
 				break;
 			}
 		});
 
 		function set_page() {
 			$ui.find(".page > .current").text(lSlider.getCurrentSlideCount()).end()
 			.find(".page > .total").text(lSlider.getTotalSlideCount());
 		}
 
 	});
 	// 메인 띠배너 롤링
 
 
 	// 메인 MD추천
 	$(".main-md").each(function() {
 
 		var $ui = $(this);
 		var $tabItem = $ui.find(".tabmenu li");
 		var $listItem = $ui.find(".list ul");
 
 		$tabItem.on("click", function(_e) {
 			_e.preventDefault();
 			var index = $tabItem.index(this);
 			$tabItem.removeClass("on").children("a").removeAttr("title").end()
 			.eq(index).addClass("on").children("a").attr("title", "선택됨");
 			$listItem.removeClass("on").eq(index).addClass("on");
 		});
 
 	});
 	// 메인 MD추천
 
 
 	// 이미지 프리로드
 	$("[data-src]").each(function() {
 		var $this = $(this);
 		var imgUrl = $this.data("src");
 		var img = new Image();
 		img.onload = function() {
 			$this.attr("src", imgUrl);
 		}
 		img.src = imgUrl;
 		$this.removeAttr("data-src");
 	});
 
 
 	// 모달윈도우
 	launchWindow('#dialog');
 
 	$('#modal_pop .close').click(function () {
 	$('#mask').hide();
 	$('#dialog').hide();
 });
 
 $(window).resize(function () {
 	var box = $('#modal_pop #dialog');
 	var maskHeight = $(document).height();
 	var maskWidth = $(window).width();
 	$('#mask').css({'width':maskWidth,'height':maskHeight});
 
 	var winH = $(window).height();
 	var winW = $(window).width();
 	box.css('top', winH/2 - box.height()/2);
 	box.css('left', winW/2 - box.width()/2);
 	});
 });
 
 function launchWindow(id) {
 	var maskHeight = $(document).height();
 	var maskWidth = $(window).width();
 	$('#mask').css({'width':maskWidth,'height':maskHeight});
 	$('#mask').fadeIn(10);
 	$('#mask').fadeTo("slow",0.50);	//배경밝기
 
 	var winH = $(window).height();
 	var winW = $(window).width();
 	$(id).css('top', winH/2 - $(id).height()/2);
 	$(id).css('left', winW/2-$(id).width()/2);
 	$(id).fadeIn(10);
 }
   </script>
  </head>

     <!-- 최근본상품

   <!-- // 201708 개편 - 오른쪽윙(바로패플, 최근본상품, 위로/아래로) -->
   <script>
    movelist("default");
 //20170907 구기원 최근본상품 페이징 및 리스트구성
 function movelist(mode){
 var makehtml="";
 
 var arr_goods_idx = new Array();
 var arr_goods_id = new Array();
 var arr_goods_no = new Array();
 var arr_goods_name = new Array();
 var arr_goods_price = new Array();
 var move_step;
 
 
 
 if(localStorage.getItem("stoidx") != null){
 	arr_goods_idx = localStorage.getItem("stoidx").split("§");
 }
 if(localStorage.getItem("stogoods_id") != null){
 	arr_goods_id = localStorage.getItem("stogoods_id").split("§");
 }
 if(localStorage.getItem("stogoods_no") != null){
 	arr_goods_no = localStorage.getItem("stogoods_no").split("§");
 }
 if(localStorage.getItem("stogoods_name") != null){
 	arr_goods_name = localStorage.getItem("stogoods_name").split("§");
 }
 if(localStorage.getItem("stoprice") != null){
 	arr_goods_price = localStorage.getItem("stoprice").split("§");
 }
 
 
 var total_goods = arr_goods_id.length-1
 var max_page = Math.ceil(total_goods/3);
 if (max_page == 0) max_page = 1;
 if (total_goods < 4) $("#id_control").hide();
 
 if (mode == "prev"){
 	if(Number($("#goods_move_step").val()) > 1 ){
 		val = Number($("#goods_move_step").val())- 1
 	}else{
 		return;
 	}
 }
 else if(mode == "next"){
 	if(Number($("#goods_move_step").val()) < max_page){
 		val = Number($("#goods_move_step").val())+ 1
 	}else{
 		return;
 	}
 }
 else if(mode == "default"){
 		val = 1;
 }
 //데이터갱신용 - 삭제시
 else{
 	val = $("#goods_move_step").val();
 	//상품이 적은데 페이지에 머물러있으면 안되니까 처리.
 	if (val > 1){
 		if (total_goods == (val-1) * 3){
 			val = val - 1;
 		}
 	}
 }
 $("#id_total").text(max_page);
 $("#id_totalcnt").text("("+total_goods+")");
 $("#id_current").text(val);
 $("#goods_move_step").val(val);
 
 move_step = val;
 //페이징관련.
 var start_num = ((Number(move_step)-1) * 3) + 1;
 var end_num = start_num + 3;
 
 //페이지가 총 상품개수보다 많을경우 최대값줄여준다.
 if (arr_goods_no.length < end_num){
 	end_num = arr_goods_no.length
 }
 for(var i = start_num; i <end_num ; i++){
 
 makehtml = makehtml + "<ul style='display:block'>";
 makehtml = makehtml +	 "<li>";
 makehtml = makehtml +		"<div class='list-item'>";
 makehtml = makehtml +			"<a href='/mall/goods/goods.asp?goods_id="+arr_goods_id[i]+"'>";
 makehtml = makehtml +				"<div class='img'>"
 makehtml = makehtml +					"<img src='http://img.fashionplus.co.kr/mall/assets/product_img/" + arr_goods_no[i].split("_")[0] + "/plg" + arr_goods_no[i] + ".jpg?resizewb=100x100' alt='최근본상품'>";
 makehtml = makehtml +				"</div>"
 makehtml = makehtml +				"<div class='caption'>";
 makehtml = makehtml +					"<p class='item_name'>"+arr_goods_name[i]+"</p>";
 //makehtml = makehtml +					"<p class='item_price'>"+arr_goods_price[i]+"원</p>";
 makehtml = makehtml +				"</div>";
 makehtml = makehtml +			"</a>";
 makehtml = makehtml +			"<button class='btn_delete' type='button' title='삭제' onclick='ajax_refrash_list("+arr_goods_id[i]+")'><span>&times;</span></button>";							
 makehtml = makehtml +		"</div>";
 makehtml = makehtml +	"</li>";
 makehtml = makehtml + "</ul>";
 
 }
 
 $("#id_list").html(makehtml);
 
 }
 
 function ajax_refrash_list(del_goods_id){
 $.ajax({
 	type:"post",
 	url:"/mall/goods/ajax_refresh_list.asp?del_goods_id="+del_goods_id,
 	data:"",
 	dateType:"json",
 	error:function(){
 		alert("err");
 		return false;
 	},
 success:function(JsonData){
 	if (JsonData != ""){
 		var evalData = eval('(' + JsonData + ')');
 		with(evalData.result){
 			localStorage.removeItem("stoidx")
 			localStorage.removeItem("stogoods_id")
 			localStorage.removeItem("stogoods_no")
 			localStorage.removeItem("stogoods_name")
 			localStorage.removeItem("stoprice")
 
 			localStorage.setItem("stoidx",arr_idx);
 			localStorage.setItem("stogoods_id",arr_goods_id);
 			localStorage.setItem("stogoods_no",arr_goods_no);
 			localStorage.setItem("stogoods_name",arr_goods_name);
 			localStorage.setItem("stoprice",arr_price);
 			
 			movelist();
 		}
 	}
 }
 });
 }
   </script>

      <script type="text/javascript">
       function Add_Favorite() {
 
 window.external.AddFavorite('http://www.fashionplus.co.kr/mall/default.asp?affiliate=plusFavor', '패션플러스 - 대한민국 NO.1 e-패션쇼핑몰');document.body.style.behavior='url(#default#homepage)';document.body.setHomePage('http://www.fashionplus.co.kr/mall/default.asp?affiliate=plusFavor');
 
 }
 
 function appdown(){
 var phoneNumber = document.getElementById("phone").value;
 var phoneNum1 = phoneNumber.substring(0,3);
 
 		if (phoneNumber==""){
 			alert("휴대폰 번호를 입력해 주세요.")
 		}
 		else{
 			if(phoneNum1=="010" || phoneNum1=="011" || phoneNum1=="016" || phoneNum1=="017" || phoneNum1=="018" || phoneNum1=="019"){
 			
 				if(phoneNumber.length=="10" || phoneNumber.length=="11"){
 					document.AppDownFrm.submit();
 				}
 				else{
 					alert("휴대폰 번호 형식이 잘못되었습니다.");
 				}
 			}
 			else{
 			alert("휴대폰 번호 형식이 잘못되었습니다.");
 				}
 		}
 }
 
 function onlyNumber(){
 	if ((event.keyCode<48)||(event.keyCode>57)){
 		event.returnValue = false;
 	}
 }
 
 function baro_login(){
 	var s = location.href
 	
 	s = s.replace("http://dv.fashionplus.co.kr","");
 	s = s.replace("http://www.fashionplus.co.kr","");
 	s = s.replace("affiliate=","affiliate_old=");
 	
 	if(confirm('바로패플 접속 이용은 로그인을 하셔야 합니다. \n지금 로그인 하시겠습니까?')){
 		location.href="/mall/login.asp?redirect_target=" + s;
 	} else {
 
 	}
 }
 
 function baro_change(){
 	document.all('iframe_change_baro').src = '/mall/include/delete_cookie.asp'
 }
      </script>

      <script type="text/javascript">
       function SelectList(frm, qty)
 {
 	document.form_search.act.value=document.form_search.Select.value;			       
 }	
 
 function ch() {
 	if( document.form_search && document.form_search.srch_word )
 		document.form_search.srch_keyword.style.backgroundImage = "";
 }
 
 var oTargetUrl;
 
 function text_check(oType){
 	//oType: 0=true, 1=submit()
 	var sKeyword;
 	
 	$("#keyword_search_table").children("li").each(function(){
 		if($(this).css("background-color")== "rgb(235, 235, 235)"){
 			$("#field_head_keyword").val($(this).text());
 		}
 	});
 
 	sKeyword = document.form_search.srch_keyword.value;
 	//sKeyword = sKeyword.replace(/\s/gi,'');
 	//sKeyword = sKeyword.replace(/ /gi,'');		
 	
 	
 	if(sKeyword == ""){
 		
 		alert("검색어를 입력해주세요.");
 		document.form_search.srch_keyword.focus();
 		return false;
 		
 	}
 	else{
 
 		try{
 			if (window.ActiveXObject){
 				oTargetUrl=new ActiveXObject("Msxml2.XMLHTTP");
 				if (! oTargetUrl){
 					oTargetUrl=new ActiveXObject("Microsoft.XMLHTTP");
 				}
 			} else if (window.XMLHttpRequest){
 				oTargetUrl=new XMLHttpRequest();
 			} 
 		//alert(sKeyword);
 			oTargetUrl.onreadystatechange = get_TargetUrl_callback;
 			oTargetUrl.open("GET", "/mall/goods/search_hot_keyword.asp?keyword=" + escape(sKeyword), true);
 			oTargetUrl.send();
 		}catch (err){
 
 		}
 		if(oTargetUrl.readyState == 1){   
 			if(oType==1){document.form_search.submit();}
 		}
 		if(oTargetUrl.readyState == 4){   
 			if(oTargetUrl.status == 200){
 				sTargetUrl = oTargetUrl.responseText;
 				//alert(sTargetUrl);
 				if(sTargetUrl ==""){
 					if(oType==1){document.form_search.submit();}
 				}
 			}
 		}
 	}
 }
 
 
 function get_TargetUrl_callback()
 {
 	var sTargetUrl;
 	if(oTargetUrl.readyState == 4){   
 		if(oTargetUrl.status == 200){
 			sTargetUrl = oTargetUrl.responseText;
 			//alert(sTargetUrl);
 			if(sTargetUrl!=""){
 				//window.open(sTargetUrl,'HotKeyword','');
 				window.location.href = sTargetUrl;
 			}
 		}
 	}	
 }
 
 function fnAutoCompleteSearch(srchWord){
 	location.href="/mall/goods/search_list.asp?search_type=text&act=&srch_keyword=" + srchWord;
 }
 
 function search_clear_text() {
 	if($("#field_head_keyword")[0]){
 		$("#field_head_keyword").val("").focus();
 		check_clear_button();
 		$("#keyword_search_table").html("").hide();
 	}
 }
 
 function check_clear_button() {
 	// 검색어 삭제버튼 노출 확인
 	if (document.form_search.srch_keyword.value.length > 0) $("#new_header .searchfield .btn_remove").show();
 	else $("#new_header .searchfield .btn_remove").hide();
 }
 
 $(function() {
 
 	var $keyword = $("#field_head_keyword");
 	var $keywordTable = $("#keyword_search_table");
 
 	if($keyword[0]){
 		$keyword.val("아디다스 키즈 여름샌들 2만원대~!").data("isInit", true);//isInit은 초기 검색어 세팅 검사 시 사용
 		$keyword.one("focusin", function() {
 			search_clear_text();
 		});
 	}
 
 	$(document).on("mousedown", function(e){
 		if (!$(e.target).parents().is(".search")) {
 			$("#keyword_search_table").html("").hide();
 		}
 	});
 
 	$keyword.on("keyup", function(e){
 		check_clear_button();
 
 		var _keycode =e.keyCode;
 		var _color = "rgb(235, 235, 235)";	
 		var _idx = -1;
 		var _length = 0;
 		
 		if(_keycode == 38 || _keycode == 40){
 			
 			_length = $("#keyword_search_table").children("li").length -1;
 
 			$("#keyword_search_table").children("li").each(function(){
 				if($(this).css("background-color")==_color){
 					_idx =$(this).index();
 					$(this).css("background-color", "");
 				}
 			});
 
 			if(_keycode == 38){
 				if(_idx == 0 || _idx == -1){
 					_idx = _length;
 				}
 				else{
 					_idx += -1;
 				}
 			}
 			else{
 				if(_idx == _length){
 					_idx = 0;
 				}
 				else{
 					_idx += 1;
 				}
 			}
 
 			$("#keyword_search_table").children("li").eq(_idx).css("background-color", _color);
 
 			return false;
 		}
 
 		// 자동완성 리스트는 최대 10개까지 노출합니다.
 		// 기존 스크립트 및 불러오는 부분을 변경된 코드에 맞게 변경하여 적용했습니다.
 		$.ajax({
 			type: "POST",
 			url: "/mall/goods/search_autocomplete_word_ansi.asp",
 			data: "autoWord=" + escape($.trim($("#field_head_keyword").val())),
 			datatype: "html",
 			success: function (responseText) {
 				if (responseText != "fail") {
 					$keywordTable.html("");
 					$($.parseHTML(responseText).slice(0, 10)).each(function(i) {
 						var $data = $(this);
 						$('<li>'
 						+'<a href="/mall/goods/search_list.asp?search_type=text&act=&srch_keyword=' + $data.attr("onclick").split('\'')[1] + '">'
 						+ $data.find("p").html()
 						+'</a>'
 						+'</li>').appendTo($keywordTable);
 					});
 					$keywordTable.show();
 				} else {
 					$keywordTable.html("").hide();
 				}
 			},
 			error: function (responseText) {
 				$keywordTable.html("").hide();
 			}
 		});
 	});
     /*20180405 mstar*/
     var best_slide = $("#best-slide").lightSlider({
         item: 1,
         loop: true,
         pause: 4000,
         slideMargin:0,
         pager: false,
         controls: false,
         auto: false,
         pauseOnHover:false,
         enableTouch:true,
         enableDrag:true,
     });
 
     $('.best100-top').find(".lSPrev").on("click", function(_e) {
         _e.preventDefault();
         best_slide.goToPrevSlide();
     });
 
     $('.best100-top').find(".lSNext").on("click", function(_e) {
         _e.preventDefault();
         best_slide.goToNextSlide();
     });
 	/* // 20180405 mstar*/
 
     /*20180330 mstar*/
 	var mdchoiceSlider = $("#mdchoice-slide").lightSlider({
 		item: 1,
 		loop: true,
 		pause: 4000,
 		slideMargin:0,
 		pager: false,
 		controls: false,
 		auto: false,
 		pauseOnHover:false,
 		enableTouch:true,
 		enableDrag:true,
 		/*20180620 mstar md초이스 비활성화시 영역 삭제*/
 		onSliderLoad: function (el) {
 			if(el.getTotalSlideCount() === 0 || el[0].childElementCount === 0){
 				//MD CHOICE를 비활성화 하여 ul에 슬라이드 li가 없을경우 md choice영역 삭제
 				$('.mdchoice').remove();
 			}else if (el.getTotalSlideCount() === 1) {
 				// 슬라이드가 총 1개만 들어가있을 경우 페이징 표시 삭제
 				$('.mdchoice .currentPager').remove();
 			}else{
 				$('#current').text(el.getCurrentSlideCount());
 				$('#total').text(el.getTotalSlideCount());
 			}
 		},
 		/*20180620 mstar*/
 		onBeforeSlide: function (el) {
 			$('#current').text(el.getCurrentSlideCount());
 		}
 	});
 	$('.mdchoice').find(".lsPrev").on("click", function(_e) {
 		_e.preventDefault();
 		mdchoiceSlider.goToPrevSlide();
 	});
 	$('.mdchoice').find(".lsNext").on("click", function(_e) {
 		_e.preventDefault();
 		mdchoiceSlider.goToNextSlide();
 	});
 
 	var themegroupSlider = $("#themegroup-slide").lightSlider({
 		item: 1,
 		loop: true,
 		pause: 4000,
 		slideMargin:0,
 		pager: false,
 		controls: true,
 		auto: true,
 		pauseOnHover:false,
 		enableTouch:true,
 		enableDrag:true,
 	});
 
     $('.bestseller-tab li').click(function(){
 		$('.bestseller-tab li').removeClass('current');
 		$(this).addClass('current');
 		var tab_index = $(this).index();
 		$('#eventlist .evetlist_wrap').removeClass('current');
 		$('.tab0'+(tab_index+1)+'-bind').addClass('current');
 	});
 	/*20180330 mstar*/
 
     /*20180531 mstar 바캉스 서브 상품리스트 탭*/
 	$('.subtheme-cate-tab li').click(function(){
 		$('.subtheme-cate-tab li').removeClass('current');
 		$('#eventlist .evetlist_wrap').removeClass('current');
 		$(this).addClass('current');
 		var tab_index = $(this).index();
 		if($(this).parent('ul').attr('class').indexOf('tab02') >= 0) tab_index = tab_index+7
 		$($('#eventlist .evetlist_wrap')[tab_index]).addClass('current');
 	});
 	/*20180531 mstar*/
 
     /*20180524 mstar*/
 	// 착한마켓 메인 롤링 슬라이더
 	$(".goodmarket-slide").each(function() {
 		var $ui = $(this);
 		var lSlider = $ui.children("ul").lightSlider({
 			item: 1,
 			loop: true,
 			pause: 4000,
 			slideMargin:0,
 			pager: false,
 			controls: true,
 			auto: true,
 			pauseOnHover:false,
 			enableTouch:true,
 			enableDrag:true,
 		});
 		$ui.find(".btn_prev").on("click", function(_e) {
 			_e.preventDefault();
 			lSlider.goToPrevSlide();
 		});
 
 		$ui.find(".btn_next").on("click", function(_e) {
 			_e.preventDefault();
 			lSlider.goToNextSlide();
 		});
         if(lSlider[0].childElementCount === 1) $('.market-slide-control').remove(); //20180531 mstar
 	});
 
 	// 메인 띠배너 롤링
 	$(".goodmarket-slide-banner").each(function() {
 		var $ui = $(this);
         /* 20180531 mstar*/
 		if($ui.children("ul")[0].childElementCount === 0) {
 			$('.goodmarket-slide-banner').remove();
 			return false;
 		}
 		if($ui.children("ul")[0].childElementCount === 1) $('.goodmarket-slide-banner').find('.control').remove();
 		/* // 20180531 mstar*/
 		var lSlider = $ui.children("ul").lightSlider({
 			item: 1,
 			mode: "fade",
 			loop: true,
 			pager: false,
 			controls: false,
 			auto: true,
 			pause: 3000,
 			//pauseOnHover:true,
 			enableTouch:false,
 			enableDrag:false,
 			onSliderLoad: set_page,
 			onBeforeSlide: set_page
 		});
 
 		$ui.find(".btn_prev").on("click", function(_e) {
 			_e.preventDefault();
 			lSlider.goToPrevSlide();
 		});
 
 		$ui.find(".btn_next").on("click", function(_e) {
 			_e.preventDefault();
 			lSlider.goToNextSlide();
 		});
 
 		$ui.find(".btn_toggle").on("click", function(_e) {
 			_e.preventDefault();
 			$(this).toggleClass("on");
 			if ($(this).hasClass("on")) lSlider.pause();
 			else {
 				lSlider.goToPrevSlide();
 				lSlider.play();
 			}
 		});
 
 		$ui.on("mouseenter mouseleave", function(_e) {
 			switch(_e.type) {
 				case "mouseenter":
 					lSlider.pause();
 				break;
 				case "mouseleave":
 					if (!$ui.find(".btn_toggle").hasClass("on")) {
 						lSlider.goToPrevSlide();
 						lSlider.play();
 					}
 				break;
 			}
 		});
 		function set_page() {
 			$ui.find(".page > .current").text(lSlider.getCurrentSlideCount()).end()
 			.find(".page > .total").text(lSlider.getTotalSlideCount());
 		}
 	});
 
 	// 상품 BEST 탭
 	$('.goodmarket-best .category-tab li').click(function(){
 		$('.goodmarket-best .category-tab li').removeClass('current');
 		$(this).addClass('current');
 		var tab_index = $(this).index();
 		$('#eventlist .evetlist_wrap').removeClass('current');
 		$($('#eventlist .evetlist_wrap')[tab_index]).addClass('current');
 		// $('.tab0'+(tab_index+1)+'-bind').addClass('current');
 	});
 
 	//슬라이더 마우스 오버시 컨트롤 화살표 show&hide
 	$('.goodmarket-slide').on("mouseenter mouseleave", function(_e) {
 		switch(_e.type) {
 			case "mouseenter":
 				$('.market-slide-control').children('button').show();
 			break;
 			case "mouseleave":
 				$('.market-slide-control').children('button').hide();
 			break;
 		}
 	});
 });
      </script>
